'PUBLIC NOTICE\nPOWER INTERRUPTION IN PARTS OF WESTERN, SOUTH NYANZA, \nNORTH RIFT AND CENTRAL RIFT REGIONS\nWe wish to inform our customers that power supply will be interrupted in parts of Western, South Nyanza, North Rift and Central Rift \nRegions from Friday 21st May 2021 to Sunday 23rd May 2021, to enable construction works for the proposed Olkaria-Lessos-Kibos 400kV  \nline being undertaken by the Kenya Electricity Transmission Company (KETRACO).\n\nThe power line will enhance power capacity, and improve the quality and reliability of supply in the regions.\n\nWe regret any inconvenience that may be caused during the operation.\n\nFRIDAY 21.05.2021\nTIME: 7.00 A.M. – 5.00 P.M.\n\nKAKAMEGA COUNTY\nAREA: KAKAMEGA, INGOTSE\nKakamega  Town,  Masinde  Muliro  University,  Lubao, 'POWER INTERRUPTION IN PARTS OF WESTERN AND NORTH RIFT REGIONS \n\nWe wish to inform our customers that power supply will be interrupted in parts of Western and North Rift Regions on Tuesday 25th May
